Impact medium: defensible but at the low end. Paste-a-key already works, anonymous/local-only verbs need no auth, and signup already auto-saves the key. Browser/device login is competitor-norm polish (wrangler/gh/stripe) and removes first-run friction for SSH boxes, but it is not blocking. Keep medium per the finding's own 0.6 confidence and correct sequencing note (do cheaper CLI-only wins first). |
| 10 | low | 1 | Unknown-verb resolves the single closest match but never offers ranked candidates or prefix/abbrev matching | cli/kolm.js | Extend suggestVerb to return the top 2-3 candidates within the threshold and print them as a short list; add unique-prefix resolution (if exactly one verb startsWith(cmd), dispatch it) gated so it never overrides an exact NL route. Emit the candidate list in the JSON error envelope's next[] for agents. | VERIFIED, NOT REFUTABLE. The finding's current_state is precisely accurate against the actual code. suggestVerb (cli/kolm.js:29926-29940) returns exactly ONE best Levenshtein match (threshold = max(2, floor(len/3))) and returns null otherwise. Both top-level dispatch default branches print a single guess: the table-dispatch fallback at cli/kolm.js:41320-41330 ('unknown verb' + 'did you mean: kolm <guess> ?') and the switch-default at cli/kolm.js:47512-47521 ('unknown command' + same single guess). There is NO unique-prefix subcommand resolution anywhere (no verbs.filter(v=>v.startsWith(cmd)) dispatch path — every startsWith in the file is positional-arg filtering, not verb-prefix matching) and NO multi-candidate 'did you mean' listing. The verb table / COMPLETION_VERBS list (cli/kolm.js:32813+) holds 150+ verbs, so prefix collisions the finding describes (e.g. 'comp' near compile/compute, 'de' near device/devices/demo) are plausible. The finding self-flags already_partially_present:true (the Levenshtein single-guess), which is correct.\n\nEFFORT (1 day): realistic, even slightly generous. Collecting top-N candidates within threshold + a unique-prefix check is a few dozen lines across the two dispatch sites; the repo's standing directive to skip new lock-in tests bounds test churn.\n\nIMPACT (low): accurate and the finding rates it low itself, correctly reasoning the single guess is usually right and this just removes the occasional confidently-wrong single redirect.\n\nCAVEATS: (a) Prefix resolution must be gated below the existing NL fallback at cli/kolm.js:47509 (looksLikeNaturalLanguage) so a short token like 'comp' isn't swallowed by 'ask' — the finding explicitly calls out this gating, good. (b) The proposed 'emit candidate list in the JSON error envelope's next[]' is partly aspirational: these two error branches are plain console.error with no JSON envelope today, so that sub-item is net-new scaffolding, not an extension of existing output. Minor and doesn't undermine the core finding.\n\nDefault-to-refute does not apply: there is no uncertainty here — the code unambiguously does single-guess only, with no prefix or multi-candidate behavior. Real, correctly scoped, low-impact DX upgrade. |
| 11 | low | 3.5 | No VHS .tape scripts for reproducible terminal demos of the CLI/TUI | scripts/, public/ | Add scripts/demos/*.tape for the marquee flows (quickstart, compile, tui, doctor) and a `make demos` (or release-verify gate) that re-records GIFs with VHS so the website transcripts always match shipped behavior. Confirmed the two existing terminal-demo paths are both hand-authored and disconnected from real CLI/TUI output: (1) C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/scripts/video/gen-demo-video.mjs hard-codes every CLI command and output line in a SCENES array fed to ffmpeg drawtext — no kolm process is ever invoked; (2) C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/scripts/build-tui-demo-cast.mjs generates public/cdn/kolm-assets/tui-demo.cast from hand-typed template-literal pane layouts and status-bar strings — its own header comment calls it the "Source-of-truth ... when the demo storyboard changes", i.e. a manual storyboard, not a capture of `kolm tui`. So the technique (VHS-scripted, reproducible, golden-file-capable terminal recordings) is genuinely absent.  Adjustments: impact is correctly "low" — this is marketing/docs accuracy plus a novel TUI regression angle, not core DX; kolm's actual users (solo devs, ML engineers, enterprise) run the CLI and never consume .tape files, so leverage accrues to the kolm team's own docs, not end users. Effort is underestimated: the dev environment is Windows (gen-demo-video.mjs hardcodes a winget ffmpeg path), and VHS depends on ttyd which is Linux/macOS-first and awkward on Windows — an unstated prerequisite. Also the CLI has interactive auth/login and non-deterministic output (latencies, ids, timestamps) that must be seeded/scrubbed before recordings are stable enough for golden-file regression. Realistic effort is ~3-4 days, not 2. |

**Planned action items:**
- [critical, 2d] **Honor --json in the global error catch (dual-consumer envelope) (GAP)** — main() global catch (~47525) always emits plain stderr text regardless of --json; detect --json/KOLM_OUTPUT=json and emit the existing jsonErrorEnvelope() (wired into only ~6 sites) with a stable KOLM_E_* code + suggested_fix/next[]. Agents/CI get clean JSON on success but unparseable text on failure today. _(cli/kolm.js)_
- [high, 3d] **Wire rejectUnknownFlags across high-traffic verbs (BUG)** — rejectUnknownFlags (sound, with 'did you mean') has exactly ONE caller (cmdCompute); a typo'd --jsno is silently dropped on ~150 verbs. Add a per-verb ALLOWED_FLAGS map called centrally from withErrorContext/_dispatchVerb; start with compile/run/distill/doctor/export/deploy/whoami/config; global flags always allowed. _(cli/kolm.js)_
- [high, 3d] **Dynamic shell completion of artifact IDs/namespaces/enums (FRONTIER)** — Hidden kolm __complete <line> printing live candidates; rewrite bash/zsh/fish emitters to delegate for arg positions (*.kolm after inspect/run/fix, --target export enum, --namespace known namespaces, recipe names); keep static fallback offline. Data already exists; thin shim. _(cli/kolm.js)_
- [high, 5d] **Multi-step plan execution with per-step confirm (Warp Agent-mode) (FRONTIER)** — kolm do --plan returns ordered steps[]{command,why,destructive}; print plan then execute [y/e/s/q] per step (auto-confirm read-only, always-prompt destructive); reuse classifyIntent; --yes for non-interactive, respect KOLM_NO_INTERACTIVE; single-shot cmdDo stays default. _(cli/kolm.js, src/intent.js)_ · depends: Honor --json in the global error catch (dual-consumer envelope) (GAP)
- [medium, 1d] **Grow errorHint into a contextual remediation registry (UPGRADE)** — errorHint covers only 4 patterns; add ordered {matcher,hint,next[]} for network/timeout/402-plan-gate/429-rate-limit/missing-toolchain/CUDA-VRAM-OOM/ENOENT; feed the same next[] into jsonErrorEnvelope so human + agent get identical remediation. Reinforces the dual-consumer envelope. _(cli/kolm.js)_ · depends: Honor --json in the global error catch (dual-consumer envelope) (GAP)
- [medium, 1d] **Passive update-notifier (UPGRADE)** — Once-per-24h cached version check (timestamp in ~/.kolm) printing a boxed 'kolm X.Y available — run kolm update' on the NEXT run; unref'd fetch (no startup latency); gate on TTY + NO_UPDATE_NOTIFIER + KOLM_NO_PROGRESS so CI/pipes stay silent. Reuse cmdUpgrade's 5s-timeout fetch. _(cli/kolm.js)_
- [medium, 2d] **kolm explain <KOLM_E_code> long-form error reference (UPGRADE)** — ERROR_CODES map {code->{title,detail,fix,docs_url}}; kolm explain KOLM_E_... expands a code; include code in every human+JSON error + a 'run kolm explain <code>' breadcrumb; audit so every thrown error carries a code. Compounds with the dual-consumer envelope (same taxonomy). _(cli/kolm.js)_ · depends: Honor --json in the global error catch (dual-consumer envelope) (GAP)
- [medium, 3d] **Self-healing doctor --fix beyond seed generation (UPGRADE)** — A fixer per doctor check (mkdir ~/.kolm, write default config.toml, install completion, clear rejected token) keyed by check id; doctor --fix iterates auto-fixable checks, --dry-run previews exact commands, --yes applies; non-mechanical checks stay guidance only. _(cli/kolm.js)_

Requires ttyd+ffmpeg (dev-toolchain, not runtime). _(scripts/, public/)_

### Run / Serve & Deploy  `run`

_9 verified findings (1 critical, 2 high)._

**Audit summary.** The Run/Serve & Deploy surface is structurally solid and unit-tested: serve auto-detect (gguf->llama.cpp / safetensors->vllm\|mlx) is a clean pure decision table wired into the CLI; deploy generators (docker-compose, k8s, vLLM config, deterministic air-gap tar.gz with offline verifier) are real and green; hardware detection has an honest CPU floor; remote-compute catalog + launch-plan builders are correct; the quantize worker isolates heavy ML deps with per-method doctor gating and a real 724-line quantize.py. The largest substantive gap: NO production path ever produces a measured ('tested') runtime passport — the referenced apps/export/probe.py does not exist, so recordTestedPassport and all v2 enrichment helpers are unit-test-only and every artifact ships estimate-only performance rows. Secondary issues: a self-contradicting exllamav2 path inside serve-autodetect.js, two divergent docker/k8s generators, willArtifactFit is a stub, serve doesn't pre-check artifact existence, the /bin/false fallback is non-portable on Windows, and the remote-compute catalog is hard-coded/unverified. Tests: r1/r3/r4/wave250 = 74 pass / 0 fail / 1 skip; deploy/airgap suites = 77 pass / 1 fail (cosmetic stale sw.js cache-token assertion only, not a functional regression). Full result written to C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/audit/w920/run.audit.json."

**Audit-flagged gaps:**
- No production path produces a status='tested' runtime passport: recordTestedPassport + generateRuntimePassport v2 helpers exist and are unit-tested, but the only named caller (apps/export/probe.py) does not exist on disk. Every shipped artifact carries only 'estimated' rows, so inspect-UI latency/tok_s/memory are model-derived estimates, never measured.
- exllamav2 runtime drift inside serve-autodetect.js: selectRuntime()/RUNTIME_SELECTION can return runtime:'exllamav2' but KNOWN_RUNTIMES + buildCommand() cannot boot it (falls to /bin/false). Same-file contradiction the header warns about.
- kolm serve never fs.existsSync()-checks the model artifact file before spawning; a bad path fails opaquely in the child process instead of a clean NOT_FOUND.
- buildCommand() '/bin/false' fallback is non-portable on Windows serve hosts.
- Two independent docker-compose + k8s generators (serve-autodetect.js vs deploy-generators.js) with different image refs (ggerganov vs ggml-org), ports (8788 vs 8000), structure — duplicate sources of truth.
- willArtifactFit() is a stub: ignores the artifact path (TODO W873) and returns a coarse vram>=4 && !cpu heuristic.
- Air-gap bundle is not self-contained: vllm wheelhouse / llama.cpp binary must be pre-staged on an internet box; installer exits 1 otherwise.
- remote-compute catalog hard-coded with verified_at=_UNVERIFIED (2026-05-18) for all 9 providers; pricing/model lists have no freshness mechanism.
- Out-of-the-box local quantize does nothing until the operator manually builds a venv + installs requirements.txt (by-design isolation, real first-run friction).
- v2 passport sub-objects (kv_cache/speculative_decoding/prompt_cache/continuous_batching) have attach helpers but no integration that populates them on a real manifest.

| 4 | low | 0.5 | kolm serve never fs.existsSync(artifact) before spawning the runtime child, and buildCommand falls back to /bin/false on unmapped runtimes, both producing opaque failures, worst on Windows | cli/kolm.js, src/serve-autodetect.js | Add fs.existsSync(ap) up front in cmdServe -> exit EXIT.NOT_FOUND with the resolved path. I verified the actual code at C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/cli/kolm.js and C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/src/serve-autodetect.js.  (1) MISSING fs.existsSync(ap) — REAL. _cmdServeAutodetect (cli/kolm.js:13895-14077) resolves ap at 13907, reads only the OPTIONAL sidecar (13945 is the single existsSync in the whole function, on ap+'.manifest.json'), runs detectRuntime, then spawns the child at 14062 with no stat of the model file. The file header (152-154) already documents this as a known drift hazard. | 5 | low | 3.5 | No multi-LoRA / batched-LoRA kernel awareness; deploy quantization config doesn't steer vLLM toward Marlin/Machete W4A16 kernels | src/forge-fit.js, src/deploy-generators.js, src/runtime-passport.js | Add kernel-awareness to forge-fit ranking and the runtime passport: for awq/gptq-4bit on Ampere+/Hopper, annotate 'marlin-eligible'/'machete-eligible' and surface it in the serve banner + deploy README. Confirmed across all relevant layers: (1) src/forge-fit.js QUALITY_ORDER ranks awq-4bit/gptq-4bit (lines 114-118) with no kernel notion; (2) src/deploy-generators.js generateVllmConfig (line 458) passes `quantization` straight through with no kernel/Marlin steering, and is not even referenced from router.js; (3) src/runtime-passport.js has rich v2 enrichment (kv_cache/speculative_decoding/prompt_cache/continuous_batching) but NO kernel-eligibility field; (4) src/quantization-oracle.js tracks `runtimes` per method but no kernel selection; (5) apps/runtime/serve.py never sets a `quantization=` kwarg at all and has zero marlin/machete reference. src/kernel-selector.js EXISTS but is unrelated — it picks latency-vs-batching workload profiles, not GEMM kernels. So already_partially_present:false is accurate.  IMPACT IS OVERBLOWN — downgrade medium->low. The "up to ~10x slower" / "2.6-10.9x left on the table" headline does not reflect the real user scenario. You generally do NOT need to set quantization:'gptq_marlin' manually. The 67->741 tok/s number is the Marlin-vs-no-Marlin delta, not "kolm's config vs ideal" on current vLLM. The real residual value is the annotation/credibility surface (proving the artifact is Marlin-eligible, fitting kolm's receipt ethos) plus a safety-net explicit hint for older vLLM / non-standard packing — genuine but worth far less than the cited multipliers. It also overlaps heavily with the sibling finding in this same audit about deploy-config drift (FP8 KV-cache + prefix-cache parity), which is the higher-value config-parity work and largely subsumes the kernel-hint piece.  EFFORT roughly right, slightly low at 3 days. The hard part is a correct kernel-eligibility predicate (Marlin sm80+, Machete sm90, plus group-size/act-order packing constraints) without overclaiming — not the trivial "awq/gptq on Ampere+" the proposal implies. ~3.5 days with tests.  Verdict: real, not already present, but a low-impact polish/annotation item (not a frontier throughput unlock) because the underlying kernel speedup is already delivered by vLLM auto-detection. |
| 6 | low | 10 | Disaggregated prefill/decode (disagg.py) is fully designed with a spec schema but never wired into serve or deploy generators | apps/runtime/serve.py, apps/runtime/disagg.py, src/deploy-generators.js | Phase 1 (cheap): wire INPROC disagg into serve.py when >=2 local GPUs and the artifact carries serve.disagg.mode=inproc, passing disagg.py engine kwargs straight through. ### Govern / Receipts & Compliance  `govern`

_10 verified findings (0 critical, 3 high)._

**Audit summary.** The Govern / Receipts & Compliance surface is substantially implemented and well-tested at the unit level. All 9 audited modules (gateway-receipt, receipt-schema, evidence-dag, assurance-case, drift-detector, cost-displacement, artifact-lifecycle, provenance, audit) export their headline symbols, are wired into router.js endpoints (/v1/verify, /v1/receipts/*, /v1/evidence/*, /v1/assurance/*, /v1/artifacts/:id/lifecycle, /v1/audit/*, /v1/savings/displacement, /v1/drift/status), and their dedicated suites pass (r2/r5/r6/r7/r8 + wrapper-r1-r8 + wrapper-receipt-schema + wave888i-receipt-export + wave770/wave448 = all green; 115 tests across the runs I executed). Real cryptography is present: Ed25519 public-key receipt signing/verification (closing the historical 2026-05-12 gap), HMAC-chained append-only audit log with tamper-evident verification, and an honestly-scoped provenance credential schema that explicitly avoids C2PA conformance claims. The modules are disciplined about never fabricating evidence (assurance-case downgrades with limitations; drift refuses thin baselines; cost-displacement flags unrepriced rows). The most material finding is an end-to-end wiring gap: both the drift detector's fallback-rate signal and cost-displacement's counterfactual branch on a route_decision value 'frontier_fallback' the receipt builder can never emit (it coerces to local\|frontier), so on production observation rows that signal is inert -- the unit tests miss this because they inject the value directly. A related latent schema-drift risk is gateway-router emitting fallback_reason values outside the receipt FALLBACK_REASONS enum. Secondary items: lifecycle side-effect hooks are in-memory stubs, two divergent lifecycle transition tables, and the public verify endpoint exposing cost/token/namespace fields to anonymous callers. No fabricated functionality found; gaps are integration/wiring and tech-debt, not missing features. Full result written to C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/audit/w920/govern.audit.json.

**Audit-flagged gaps:**
- INTEGRATION: drift-detector fallback_rate_delta and cost-displacement frontier_fallback branch read a route_decision value ('frontier_fallback') the receipt builder/observation writer never emits (only local\|frontier). On production data the headline drift fallback signal is structurally ~0; the real fallback signal is in the separate fallback_reason field. Unit tests pass only because fixtures inject the value directly.
- SCHEMA DRIFT: gateway-router.js emits fallback_reason values 'empty_chain' and 'low_confidence_prior' absent from FALLBACK_REASONS; if they reach buildAndSignReceipt they fail validation and abort the call.
- STUB: artifact-lifecycle blockPulls/alertDeployments/linkSuccessor are in-memory no-op logs not wired to a durable subscriber/alert ladder; log resets per process.
- TECH DEBT: two lifecycle transition tables (TRANSITIONS vs VALID_TRANSITIONS) with different legal moves; drift_detected/re_evaluated states are not in LIFECYCLE_STATES.
- DESIGN DECISION NEEDED: public /v1/verify/:receipt_id returns cost_usd, token counts, namespace_id, provider, model to unauthenticated callers via a global all('observations') scan.
- DOC INCONSISTENCY (minor): receipt-schema.js header says hashes are 'kept short (16 hex)' but _sha256Short produces 32 hex; regex allows 16-64 so harmless, but the comment is wrong.

| # | Impact | Eff(d) | Finding | Files | Change | Verify note |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | high | 1.5 | frontier_fallback route_decision consumers are dead code on real receipts | src/drift-detector.js, src/cost-displacement.js, tests/r7-drift-detector.test.js, tests/r8-cost-displacement.test.js | Pick one representation. Recommended: keep route_decision two-valued and rewrite _fallbackRate() and cost-displacement to count fallbacks as route_decision==='frontier' AND fallback_reason!=null (rows already persist fallback_reason at router.js:6407). Update r7/r8 fixtures to the real persisted shape so the test exercises the production path. | CONFIRMED REAL — not refuted. Verified every claim against the actual code.  MECHANISM (all confirmed): - src/receipt-schema.js:83: `ROUTE_DECISIONS = Object.freeze(['local','frontier'])`. validateReceipt (line 147-148) rejects any other value. - src/gateway-receipt.js:110: `r.route_decision = opts.route_decision === 'local' ? 'local' : 'frontier'` — hard coercion. The signed receipt can NEVER carry 'frontier_fallback'. - src/router.js:6354: a real local->frontier fallback sets `fallback_reason` (non-null) when attempted.length > 1; line 6358 resolves route_decision to 'frontier'. Persisted at router.js:6406 (route_decision) + 6407 (fallback_reason) as SEPARATE fields on the observations row. - src/runtime-policy.js:467 `reason:'frontier_fallback'` is a decision REASON string, not a route_decision — it does not rescue the consumers.  DEAD CODE (confirmed): - src/drift-detector.js:277 `_fallbackRate` counts only `route_decision==='frontier_fallback'`. On real observation rows this is always 0, so fallback_rate is structurally 0 and fallback_rate_delta is structurally 0/null. This is a HEADLINE signal: drift-detector.js:21 lists it as signal #1 and SEVERITY_THRESHOLDS.high_fallback_rate_delta=0.05 (line 640) escalates drift to 'high' — so the escalation is effectively disabled in production. - src/cost-displacement.js:297 the `frontier_fallback` branch never fires on real data; a real fallback (route_decision='frontier') instead lands in the 'frontier' branch (line 293) and is counted as frontierCount. So frontier_fallback_count (line 384) is always 0 in the operator-facing cost report.  WHY TESTS PASS (confirmed): r7/r8 fixtures build raw row objects via local helpers (r8 rec() at tests/r8-cost-displacement.test.js:37-50; r7 receipt() at :34) that bypass buildAndSignReceipt and set route_decision:'frontier_fallback' directly (r7 lines 110/123/189/238/364; r8 line 98 with assert frontier_fallback_count==1 at :124). They exercise a shape production cannot emit.  ALREADY IMPLEMENTED? No. This is a latent correctness bug, not a shipped/intentional feature. The only occurrence of 'frontier_fallback' as a route_decision value in src/ is a comment (cost-displacement.js:49).  FIX FEASIBILITY: The proposed remedy is sound and the data dependency holds — drift-detector reads store.findByTenant('observations') (drift-detector.js:223), the same table the router writes fallback_reason to (router.js:6407). So rewriting the predicate to `route_decision==='frontier' && fallback_reason!=null` works with persisted data. Note: cost-displacement currently differentiates fallback (full frontier price, no displacement) from plain frontier (also no displacement) — both already add actual to baseline, so the savings math is unaffected; only the fallback BUCKET COUNT is wrong. So cost-displacement's savings number is correct; only its reporting breakdown is misattributed. Keep at 1.5.  IMPACT: high (not critical). It silently zeros two operator-facing govern signals (the drift 'traffic shifted away from artifact' escalation and the cost-report fallback bucket). The only other statistic present is histogram KL (src/drift-detect.js:220 and src/drift-detector.js:670) — not PSI, not MMD, not ADWIN.  Critically for the Govern/Compliance surface: the finding undersells the problem. The public docs page public/docs/govern/drift.html:85 already advertises "Population stability index over embedding centroids" as kolm's input-distribution statistic, and line 109 documents an `input_psi_max = 0.25` spec.toml knob — yet a strict grep shows no code ever computes PSI or parses input_psi_max anywhere in src/. So this is a live doc-vs-code gap on the exact surface a model-risk (SR 11-7) reviewer would inspect, not merely a missing nice-to-have. The 0.25 alert convention the finding cites is the same one the docs already claim.  Effort (4 days): roughly realistic, slightly optimistic at the high end. PSI is cheap (~0.5d) because the histogram-binning + KL plumbing in drift-detect.js is reusable. ADWIN is the heaviest piece (needs persisted per-namespace streaming window state with a confidence-bound shrink test — a new stateful concern vs today's stateless windowed reads) and pushes toward 4-6 days if all three land with tests + threshold calibration + SPC-ladder integration + docs reconciliation.  Impact (medium): accurate. Value concentrates in the enterprise/financial compliance segment where "what drift test do you run? PSI/MMD" is expected vocabulary; most solo/startup distill users won't ask. Medium is right.  Unstated dependencies: (1) MMD is gated on REAL embeddings — drift-detect.js accepts caller-supplied embeddings but nothing in the lake-read path produces them (the lake path uses the sha256 pseudo-embedding), so MMD would be dormant until an actual embedder is wired in. (2) Landing PSI should reconcile the already-documented-but-unparsed input_psi_max knob. (3) ADWIN needs new persisted window state. Test harness exists (tests/r7-drift-detector.test.js, tests/wave813-drift-detection.test.js), so the additions are testable. |
| 10 | low | 1 | Reconcile the two divergent lifecycle transition tables | src/artifact-lifecycle.js, tests/r2-artifact-lifecycle.test.js | Promote TRANSITIONS (the fuller R-2 ladder) to canonical, express VALID_TRANSITIONS as a derived/compat view, and make both transition() and ArtifactLifecycle.transition() validate against the same map. Add a test asserting both entry points accept exactly the same moves from every state. | VERIFIED REAL, NOT already reconciled. C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/src/artifact-lifecycle.js does contain two divergent transition tables that share the same on-disk persistence (_writeLifecycle -> lifecycle.json):  - VALID_TRANSITIONS (line 79), used by the exported transition() function (lines 167-211). signed -> [deployed, archived]; revoked -> [archived]; includes a transient 'undeployed' state; deployed -> [monitored, superseded, revoked, undeployed]. - TRANSITIONS (line 47), used by class ArtifactLifecycle.transition() (lines 353-411). signed -> [deployed, revoked] (NO signed->archived); revoked -> [] terminal; NO 'undeployed'; adds drift_detected + re_evaluated edges.  The disagreements the finding lists are accurate: signed->archived legal under VALID only; signed->revoked legal under TRANSITIONS only; revoked->archived legal under VALID only; 'undeployed' only in VALID; 'drift_detected'/'re_evaluated' only in TRANSITIONS. Both paths persist to the same lifecycle.json, so a record written by one IS read by the other — the audit-replay-ambiguity premise is sound in principle. The proposed single-canonical-map reconciliation and the cross-entry-point equivalence test do NOT exist (tests/r2-artifact-lifecycle.test.js #8 pins VALID_TRANSITIONS only; tests/wrapper-r-enrich.test.js pins TRANSITIONS separately — no test asserts the two agree).  HOWEVER the impact is correctly self-rated 'low' and the 'depending on which API the caller used' hazard is essentially latent, not active: the ArtifactLifecycle class is wired into NO production surface. Both real entry points — src/router.js (imports loadOrInit + VALID_TRANSITIONS, lines 61-68; GET /lifecycle and POST /lifecycle/transition) and cli/kolm.js (lc.loadOrInit at lines 5987-6230) — exclusively use the transition()/VALID_TRANSITIONS path. The class is constructed only in one test file (tests/wrapper-r-enrich.test.js). So today every real artifact only ever moves through one table; the second table is reachable only from a unit test. The dual-table design is also explicitly documented as intentional in the code comments (lines 41-46, 311-323): VALID_TRANSITIONS is kept as a v1 compat surface that callers pinned.  Effort 1.5d is slightly high for promoting one map to canonical + a derived compat view + one equivalence test in a ~400-line module; 1d is realistic. Real users (auditors needing one unambiguous 'allowed transitions' statement) would care in principle, but the practical exposure is near-zero until ArtifactLifecycle is actually used in production. Net: a genuine, cheap-to-close latent correctness/audit-hygiene item, correctly scoped as low impact. Not refuted. |

**Planned action items:**
- [critical, 1d] **Coerce fallback_reason at the receipt boundary (latent P0 BUG)** — dispatchWithFallback emits 'empty_chain' and selectRoute emits 'low_confidence_prior' — both outside FALLBACK_REASONS, so validateReceipt throws receipt_invalid and aborts the live call. Coerce unknown->null (or widen the enum) AND make buildAndSignReceipt coerce-with-note instead of throwing, so a logging-field bug can never take down a served request. _(src/receipt-schema.js, src/gateway-router.js, src/router.js, src/gateway-receipt.js)_
- [high, 1.5d] **Fix frontier_fallback dead branches in drift + cost-displacement (BUG)** — route_decision can only be local\|frontier, but drift fallback_rate_delta and cost-displacement bucket key on 'frontier_fallback' -> structurally ~0 on real data. Recount fallbacks as route_decision==='frontier' AND fallback_reason!=null (already on the row); update r7/r8 fixtures to the real persisted shape. _(src/drift-detector.js, src/cost-displacement.js, tests/r7-drift-detector.test.js, tests/r8-cost-displacement.test.js)_
- [high, 4d] **Transparency-log anchor PER-CALL gateway receipts (UPGRADE)** — Off-hot-path async batch-submit receipt digests to a configurable/self-hostable Rekor v2 (KOLM_SIGSTORE_REKOR_URL); store {logIndex,inclusionProof,integratedTime} on the observation row; surface from /v1/verify/:id; default dry-run/offline. Upgrades 'we signed it' to 'a log witnessed it at T'. _(src/gateway-receipt.js, src/router.js, src/sigstore.js)_ · depends: Fix RFC 6962 Merkle inclusion-proof verifier (BUG)

Answers the security-review 'where does the key live'. _(src/ed25519.js, src/gateway-receipt.js, src/audit.js)_
- [medium, 2.5d] **Wire lifecycle revoke/supersede side-effects to a durable subscriber (GAP)** — Route blockPulls/alertDeployments/linkSuccessor through a durable dispatcher: audit_events row, deployment alert via drift-alert ladder, persist successor link on lifecycle.json (survives restart); keep in-memory _sideEffectLog as a test seam only. _(src/artifact-lifecycle.js, src/audit.js, src/drift-alert.js, src/router.js)_
- [medium, 2d] **Fix RFC 6962 Merkle inclusion-proof verifier (BUG)** — Replace the hand-rolled walk with canonical RFC 9162 verify_inclusion; compare roots with a plain length-checked timingSafeEqual (no alloc/fill/slice truncation); add RFC + live-Rekor test vectors. Must be correct before live-receipt anchoring ships. _(src/sigstore.js, tests/wave150-sigstore.test.js)_
- [medium, 3d] **RFC 8785 (JCS) canonicalization for the signed payload (UPGRADE)** — Replace bespoke fixed-order JSON.stringify with RFC 8785 JCS (lexicographic sort + ECMAScript number serialization); pin cost_usd to integer micro-USD; add a cross-language conformance fixture (sign Node, verify Rust SDK) to release-verify. Makes offline verify genuinely portable. _(src/receipt-schema.js, src/cid.js, sdk/rust/src/lib.rs, sdk/c/kolm.h)_
- [medium, 4d] **PSI / MMD / ADWIN standard drift statistics (UPGRADE)** — Add PSI first-class (>0.2 warn, >0.25 alert), MMD kernel two-sample when real embeddings available, ADWIN for streaming series; keep SPC default for thin baselines. 'PSI and MMD' is the answer a model-risk reviewer expects. _(src/drift-detector.js, src/drift-detect.js, src/drift-config.js)_
- [medium, 4d] **in-toto v1 / SLSA provenance envelope for .kolm artifacts (FRONTIER)** — Wrap the existing signed payload in an in-toto v1 Statement + SLSA Provenance predicate (subject digests, materials from distill-provenance, builder.id) signed as DSSE with the same Ed25519 key; lets cosign verify-attestation/kyverno/conftest consume kolm artifacts natively. _(src/provenance.js, src/artifact.js, src/distill-provenance.js, src/sigstore.js)_

### KOLM Data Engine — Ingest / Curate / Augment (+ legacy seeds & synthetic-data)  `data-engine`

_9 verified findings (0 critical, 3 high)._

**Audit summary.** The INGEST -> CURATE -> AUGMENT core is real, runs end-to-end fully offline, and is wired to the CLI (kolm ingest/curate/augment). Live isolated-dir smokes confirmed all three stages return correct honest envelopes: ingest writes provenance-stamped raw-pairs.jsonl with id+sha256 dedupe across 6 writer paths; curate runs quality/dedup(python-degrading)/cluster/cot/pii and writes curated-pairs.jsonl; augment runs 5 templated strategies with a real cost-preview gate and preview/apply semantics. Legacy seed modules (seeds-augment, seeds-sanitize, synthetic-data) and active-learning are solid and well-tested (wave355 7/7, wave357 5/5, wave815 22/22; wave910 ingestion 12/12). The honest gaps relative to KOLM_DATA_ENGINE_PLAN.md: (1) the 6-stage ORCHESTRATOR src/data-engine.js and the planned workers/data/scripts python are NOT built — semantic dedup falls back to ngram and `kolm compile --auto` is not the full 6-stage chain; (2) NO committed tests exist for data-curate.js / data-augment.js and the engine-form ingest writers are smoke-verified only; (3) the Account UI / Data Health panel for this surface is missing (the 2 wave749 failures are these missing HTML pages); (4) --from hf and describe-teacher are export-parsers / untested-live rather than live integrations. Net: module logic = working; orchestration + python workers + UI + dedicated tests = partial/missing. Full audit JSON written to C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/audit/w920/data-engine.audit.json.

**Audit-flagged gaps:**
- src/data-engine.js orchestrator is MISSING — no single command chains INGEST->CURATE->AUGMENT->TRAIN->EVALUATE->FEEDBACK with cost gates (plan item 8 + DoD). The existing cli/kolm.js `compile --auto` is the older compile autopilot, not the 6-stage chain.
- workers/data/scripts/ python (embed_pairs/cluster_pairs/score_quality/score_failures) is MISSING — curate reuses workers/distill/scripts/dedup_pairs.py with the ngram backend (hardcoded at data-curate.js:203), so real nomic-embed semantic dedup + k-means/teacher labeling per plan C2.2/C2.3 are unbuilt.
- No committed tests for src/data-curate.js or src/data-augment.js; the engine-form ingest writers (ingestFile/From/Combined/Pairs/*Engine) are not covered by wave910-data-ingestion.test.js — they are verified only by this audit's live smoke.
- ingestFrom --from hf parses an on-disk JSONL export only; it does NOT load a HuggingFace dataset by id over the network (plan I1.8). The whole adapter family is export-file parsers, not live pulls (module-wide 'no live APIs').
- describe teacher-synthesis (synthesizeViaTeacher) is untested against a live teacher (only bootstrap fallback is covered); engine-form ingestDescribeEngine emits output:'' seeds that the curate quality gate then drops until a collect/AUGMENT step fills outputs.
- Account/front-end surface for this engine is MISSING: account/data-engine.html, account/ingest.html, the Data Health panel, and public/account\|docs/synthetic.html — the 2 failing wave749 tests are exactly these missing pages.
- Plan stages 5 (EVALUATE) and 6 (FEEDBACK) have module files present (src/data-evaluate.js, src/data-feedback.js EXIST) but were out of this audit's scope; only the AUGMENT<-FEEDBACK edge (appendFixPairs) was verified here.

IFD is a strong conceptual fit for kolm's local/no-teacher/no-embedder ethos and quality scoring is genuinely the weakest curate stage. But the headline 5-10%-of-data result is from Alpaca/WizardLM; kolm's typical corpora are small support-distill sets where aggressive IFD-band pruning may not pay off and could remove needed coverage. Unstated prerequisites: requires the base/student model to be locally loadable (config plumbing for which model + tokenizer to use), torch+transformers in the worker env, and a defined IFD band threshold per corpus — none of which exist today. Users running local distill would benefit, but the win is incremental quality-per-pair, not the transformational gain "high" implies. |

| 5 | medium | 1.5 | Real per-pair grammar/completeness/relevance signals to honour the C2.1 quality spec | src/distill-preference.js, src/data-curate.js | Extend the quality stage: (a) relevance = tokenOverlap(input, output) or embedding cosine (reuse dedup embeddings); (b) completeness = penalize outputs ending without terminal punctuation / mid-list / at the MAX_ROW_CHARS truncation boundary; (c) keep CoT/refusal. No completeness/truncation check exists. So a fluent-but-off-topic or truncated answer passes (would score ~0.4-0.55, above minQuality 0.35).  The finding's completeness premise is concretely grounded: MAX_ROW_CHARS (=32000) IS real, and docs/file ingestion TRUNCATES output via .slice(0, MAX_ROW_CHARS) (src/data-ingest.js:597, 981) — those mid-sentence-truncated chunks currently only lose 0.1 (very_long) and survive curate. No committed test pins scoreCandidateLocal's numeric scores (grep of tests/ = no matches), so extending it is low-risk.  Calibration caveats (kept impact at medium, not down to low): (1) the embedding-cosine variant of relevance is NOT free as implied — embeddings live only in the python dedup worker, not in JS at curate time, so only the deterministic tokenOverlap(input,output) variant is the no-dep option; tokenOverlap relevance is itself a crude, gameable signal. (2) Grammar/format is the weakest sub-component (regex/English-only, brittle). (3) The headline payoff 'give Data Health why-dropped UX something real' is partly latent: the audit confirms the Data Health / account UI panel is MISSING (data-engine.audit.json), so half the value waits on unbuilt UI. (4) This finding addresses the same root weakness as two sibling findings that are higher-leverage — the nomic-embedder 'bug' fix (0.5d, real semantic relevance/dedup) and the IFD difficulty score (3d, model-based) — so the marginal value over those is modest. (5) Effort 1.5d is fair for the tokenOverlap+completeness+per-pair-reason-in-report core (the quality stage currently only counts quality_filtered, so emitting per-pair component breakdown is a real but small extension); the embedding-cosine option would push it higher. Users who import messy CSV/log/docs corpora (kolm's ingest paths) would benefit from dropping off-topic and truncated pairs, so users would care — moderately.  Relevant files (absolute): C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/src/distill-preference.js (scoreCandidateLocal:220, tokenOverlap:209), C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/src/data-curate.js (quality stage:291-303), C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/src/data-ingest.js (MAX_ROW_CHARS:182, truncation:597/981, drop_long:250), C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/KOLM_DATA_ENGINE_PLAN.md (C2.1:56). |

The finding's current-state description is precisely accurate against the actual code. dedup() in C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/workers/distill/scripts/dedup_pairs.py (lines 260-298) is a greedy full-pairwise scan with no clustering: dense path grows kept_mat @ v (O(n*kept)), sparse/ngram path is an explicit nested Python for-loop over kept rows. | 7 | medium | 4 | DCLM/Nemotron-style learned quality classifier as an optional CURATE filter | src/data-curate.js, workers/data/scripts/quality_classifier.py | Add optional workers/data/scripts/quality_classifier.py: bootstrap a fastText classifier from the user's own curated-good vs filtered-bad split (or a shipped seed), score each pair, keep top fraction. **Planned action items:**
- [high, 0.5d] **Request the nomic embedder for dedup/cluster instead of hardcoded ngram (BUG)** — data-curate.js:203 hardcodes ['--embedder','ngram'] so the Node path NEVER asks for semantic dedup even when sentence-transformers is installed. Plumb an embedder choice (default 'auto'->nomic-embed-text-v1.5), rely on dedup_pairs.py's existing graceful ngram fallback; surface backend_used in the curate report. One-line capability that's silently disabled; lets the plan's curate DoD pass. _(src/data-curate.js, cli/kolm.js)_
- [high, 3d] **Model-free IFD/Superfiltering difficulty score for per-pair quality (FRONTIER)** — workers/data/scripts/score_ifd.py computing IFD = ppl(answer\|instruction)/ppl(answer) with the configured student (or gpt2 proxy on no-GPU); keep mid-high IFD band; wire as optional 'difficulty' signal in curatePairs, degrade to heuristic when torch absent (the _dedupViaPython pattern). Self-guided, needs NO teacher/embedder — best-fit frontier method; directly raises distill quality-per-pair. _(src/data-curate.js, workers/data/scripts/score_ifd.py, cli/kolm.js)_
- [high, 3d] **DEITA complexity x quality x diversity selection stage (FRONTIER)** — Add a SELECTION step to curatePairs (opts.target_size): rank by difficulty(IFD)*quality, greedily add highest-score while skipping pairs within cosine<diversity_tau of an already-selected one (reuse dedup embeddings); emit a selection report. 6K well-selected beats 60K random — directly lowers teacher spend AND raises K-Score. _(src/data-curate.js, workers/data/scripts/score_ifd.py, cli/kolm.js)_ · depends: Model-free IFD/Superfiltering difficulty score for per-pair quality (FRONTIER)
- [high, 4d] **Magpie template self-synthesis as a real AUGMENT generator (FRONTIER)** — Magpie generation mode in AUGMENT + describe-engine upgrade gated behind KOLM_TEACHER_BASE_URL (replaces empty-output template stubs): feed pre-query template to self-synthesize N domain instructions, then collect responses; reuse previewCost gate; stamp provenance.strategy='magpie'; fall back to templates with no teacher. (Same method as the studio Magpie item — single implementation.) _(src/data-augment.js, src/data-ingest.js, cli/kolm.js)_
- [medium, 2d] **Clustering-then-intra-cluster SemDeDup (scale past a few hundred pairs) (UPGRADE)** — k-means pre-cluster the (already-computed) embeddings, run the greedy threshold pass only within each cluster (near-linear vs current O(n^2)); cluster assignments double as real semantic cluster_id (replacing the 3-gram-prefix bucket). Unblocks the 10K-pair curate smoke. (Coordinate with the studio SemDedup item.) _(workers/distill/scripts/dedup_pairs.py, src/data-curate.js)_ · depends: Request the nomic embedder for dedup/cluster instead of hardcoded ngram (BUG)
- [medium, 1.5d] **Balance / distribution-skew analysis in CURATE (C2.4/C2.8) (GAP)** — After clustering, compute max:median cluster ratio -> report.balance{worst_ratio,over_represented,under_represented}; when a production_histogram is passed (already available from active-learning.detectCoverageGaps) compute per-cluster train-vs-prod skew. Mostly wiring existing sibling code so the planned Data Health Balance bar is non-cosmetic. _(src/data-curate.js)_
- [medium, 1.5d] **Real grammar/completeness/relevance quality signals (C2.1) (GAP)** — Extend the quality stage with relevance=tokenOverlap/embedding cosine(input,output), completeness=penalize truncated/mid-sentence/MAX_ROW_CHARS-boundary outputs; keep CoT/refusal; surface component breakdown so Data Health can explain WHY a pair scored low. The plan promised 5 components; only 2 ship. _(src/distill-preference.js, src/data-curate.js)_
- [medium, 3d] **DCLM/Nemotron learned quality classifier as optional CURATE filter (FRONTIER)** — Optional workers/data/scripts/quality_classifier.py: bootstrap a fastText classifier from the user's curated-good vs filtered-bad split (or shipped seed), keep top fraction; degrade to heuristic when fasttext absent. Opt-in once IFD lands (cold-start labeling is a real UX cost). _(src/data-curate.js, workers/data/scripts/quality_classifier.py)_ · depends: Model-free IFD/Superfiltering difficulty score for per-pair quality (FRONTIER)
- [medium, 3d] **Cleanlab-style label/answer-error detection (FRONTIER)** — Outlier pass: flag answers disagreeing with cluster consensus + high-loss-low-IFD answers (likely noise) as a review queue (wire existing /v1/label-queue) rather than auto-dropping. Catches 4xx-captured-as-answer bad labels in log imports. False-positive-prone -> human-in-loop. _(src/data-curate.js, workers/data/scripts/score_ifd.py)_ · depends: Model-free IFD/Superfiltering difficulty score for per-pair quality (FRONTIER)
- [low, 1.5d] **Domain-grounded personas + post-augment diversity check (UPGRADE)** — Generic-persona rewrite reduces lexical diversity vs the seed. Derive personas from the namespace's cluster labels/production traffic OR prefer Magpie and demote persona to an explicitly-marked low-diversity strategy; add a distinct-n/embedding-spread diversity-delta so the user sees whether augment actually broadened coverage. _(src/data-augment.js)_

Full DoReMi is overkill for SFT-scale; lowest priority. _(src/data-curate.js, src/data-engine.js)_ · depends: Balance / distribution-skew analysis in CURATE (C2.4/C2.8) (GAP)

### Studio / Distill & Compile  `studio`

_3 verified findings (0 critical, 2 high)._

**Audit summary.** The Distill & Compile surface is substantially production-grade. The Node distillation worker (distill.mjs) runs end-to-end in doctor/stub modes with an honest manifest, content-hash resume, cumulative cost cap, teacher-holdout scoring and a full hash receipt chain (verified live: ready_for_full_pipeline:true on a torch 2.11.0+cu128 / RTX 5090 box). The Python LoRA trainer preflights GREEN with all dependency dry-constructs passing, and supports QLoRA/NEFTune/DeepSpeed/multi-GPU+FSDP/resumable-checkpoints/reproducibility-manifest (code-complete, but the heavy paths and a real --mode=full train were not executed here — preflight only). K-score v1/v2 is complete with weight redistribution, ratio floors against false-perfect axes, and additive W810 calibration. Teacher council (W718) and council-disagreement preference mining (T2.3) are fully implemented and exercised (39 council tests + 22 disagreement-smoke checks all pass). compile.js enforces the no-seeds refusal, the pre-split-before-synthesis leakage guard, and honest artifact_class. Test suites run live: 127 unit tests + 22 smoke checks all pass; Python trainers py_compile clean. Main gaps: (1) preference RLHF training is an orchestration shell deferring to an external trainer that ships no in-repo reference; (2) the actual fine-tune and its heavy paths remain untested-at-runtime in this audit; (3) MoE recipe is an explicitly-gated scaffold with no trainer; (4) distill.mjs prints an install hint for a requirements.txt that does not exist (one concrete FAIL). Full result persisted to C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/audit/w920/studio.audit.json.

**Audit-flagged gaps:**
- Preference RLHF (DPO/SimPO/ORPO/KTO) has NO in-repo gradient implementation — src/distill-preference.js trainPreference() only orchestrates an external $KOLM_PREFERENCE_TRAINER and returns no_trainer_installed when absent; reference impls (trl/unsloth/simpo) are third-party, not bundled.
- The actual LoRA fine-tune (distill.mjs --mode=full -> train_lora.py trainer.train()) plus QLoRA NF4 / NEFTune / DeepSpeed / multi-GPU+FSDP / Unsloth paths were NOT executed in this audit — only --preflight-only ran green. Code-complete and dependency-validated but untested-at-runtime in this pass.
- MoE recipe (compile.js buildMoeRecipe) is a self-described scaffold (production_ready:false, gated behind KOLM_ENABLE_MOE) with no mixture trainer behind it.
- distill.mjs:671 instructs 'pip install -r requirements.txt' but workers/distill/requirements.txt does not exist (real dep list only in inline hint string) — minor user-facing bug.
- Recipe catalog ships a single recipe (trinity-2000); loader/dispatch is built for many but only one is present; composable-YAML DSL (T3.1) is roadmap.
- synthetic-data.js edge/counter/adversarial modes emit sentinel outputs ('__edge_case__' etc.) rather than real labels with no in-module guard against training on them directly; correctness depends on downstream teacher/gate discipline.
- T2.3 council-disagreement mining has a dedicated smoke script (scripts/t2-3-disagreement-smoke.mjs, 22 checks) but no tests/*.test.js entry, so it is excluded from the standard npm test gate.

Core claims check out against actual code: (1) `full-ft` IS in the enum (workers/distill/catalog.mjs:198) but train_lora.py:426-433 unconditionally calls get_peft_model(base, lora_cfg) with no full-fine-tune branch anywhere — selecting full-ft silently degrades to a plain LoRA fp16 train (distill.mjs:493 just omits --qlora). The enum value is genuinely non-functional. (2) GaLore is absent from all product code (no `galore`/`galore_adamw`/`optim_target_modules` token outside the audit JSON itself); src/distill-efficiency.js covers only precision/grad-ckpt/early-stop. (3) --optim passthrough exists (train_lora.py:295,483) but GaLore also needs optim_target_modules which is NOT wired, so --optim galore_adamw alone fails — finding states this correctly. (4) FSDP/multi-GPU IS shipped-but-untested: distill.mjs:515-534 builds `accelerate launch --multi_gpu --use_fsdp --fsdp_sharding_strategy=FULL_SHARD`, and no test exercises it (tests/wave727-accelerate.test.js is speculative-decoding, unrelated despite the shared word). already_partially_present:true is accurate (--optim + FSDP flags present, GaLore wiring absent), so alreadyPresent=false for the proposed GaLore/full-ft-honesty change overall. CAVEATS that reduce severity below the claimed 'medium': the Studio doc (public/docs/studio-distill.html:97) already scopes full-ft to 'rare; only for <1B', a size that fully fine-tunes on a 5090 with NO GaLore needed — so GaLore's headline (7B full-ft on 24GB) targets a use case kolm doesn't advertise. The actual defect is simpler/cheaper than the proposal: either make full-ft truly skip get_peft_model, or drop it from the enum. Unstated dependency: the proposed FSDP smoke test needs a multi-GPU box (audit confirms single-GPU reference hardware), so it can't run where it matters. Effort ~3d is plausible only if it includes the real full-ft trainer branch; adjust impact to low (most distill users want adapters; this is a narrow honesty/correctness gap on the audited surface). |

### Account UI / No-Code  `account-ui`

_9 verified findings (0 critical, 2 high)._

**Audit summary.** The account surface is a large, real product cockpit: 60 top-level pages + 18 subdir pages. The flagship console (overview.html) is genuinely data-wired against live, auth-gated tenant APIs (/v1/account, /v1/account/state, /v1/intent/next, /v1/savings/displacement, /v1/drift/status, /v1/product/graph, /v1/account/next-actions) with real skeletons, empty states, and error fallbacks. The dedicated NO-CODE builder (create-model.html) has a fully built 4-tab UI (Describe/Upload/Connect/Capture) with real client-side CSV/JSONL/JSON/TSV parsing, column auto-detection, autosave, cost estimate, and an SSE compile overlay -- BUT the compile pipeline is an explicit self-documented STUB: /v1/compile/start returns a fake cj_ job id, /v1/compile/preview returns hardcoded Q&A, and src/compile-stream.js emits 22 deterministic fake SSE events ending in a synthetic art_<jobid> slug that maps to no real artifact, so the page promise 'One outcome: a signed .kolm artifact you own' is not delivered by the no-code path. Separately there is a CSS token defect: ~42/60 pages and whats-next.js reference --good/--bad/--warn which are NOT defined in ks.css (only --green/--amber/--red/--warning exist) and live only in design-tokens.css, which 44/60 account pages do NOT load -- so status pills/dots/severity colors silently fall back to inherited ink. The wizard is also orphaned (not in the overview sidebar). Known tech debt (22 pages lack product-graph journey ownership) is already captured in docs/research/kolm-account-product-matrix-seed-2026-05-25.md. Full result written to C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/audit/w920/account-ui.audit.json.

**Audit-flagged gaps:**
- PRIMARY: The no-code Create-a-model wizard cannot produce a real .kolm artifact. /v1/compile/start, /v1/compile/preview, and the SSE stream (src/compile-stream.js) are explicit stubs emitting deterministic fake events and a synthetic art_<jobid> slug that resolves to no real artifact; the 'View artifact ->' CTA dead-ends. Contradicts the page promise 'One outcome: a signed .kolm artifact you own.'
- CSS defect: --good/--bad/--warn undefined in ks.css (only --green/--amber/--red/--warning exist). 42/60 account pages + whats-next.js reference them with no fallback, so status pills, drift dots, and severity colors silently render in inherited ink instead of green/amber/red. Fix by aliasing in ks.css or loading design-tokens.css on these pages.
- design-tokens.css (which defines --good/--bad/--warn) is loaded by only 16/60 account pages; overview.html and create-model.html are not among them.
- The no-code wizard (/account/create-model) is missing from the overview sidebar and only linked from 2 pages -- hard to discover.
- Auth-gate inconsistency: 24/60 account pages (incl create-model, members, org, gateway, sla) have no client-side signin redirect and account HTML is served statically with no server-side gate; logged-out users see bare shells that fail to populate.
- Duplicate/overlapping key pages: keys.html (static stub) and api-keys.html coexist with no clear canonical.
- 8 account pages render only static markup with no data fetch and no 'reference' classification (bakeoff, continuous-monitoring, forge, governance, keys, onboarding, pipelines, sustainability).
- Documented but unresolved: 22 account pages lack product-graph journey ownership (per docs seed); intended control file docs/account-product-matrix.json not yet built.
- Cost estimate and live-tail readiness bars are heuristic/hardcoded, not tied to real billing or capture telemetry.

| 1 | medium | 0.5 | Fix the --good/--bad/--warn CSS token defect (status colors silently dead on ~42/60 pages) | public/ks.css | Add to ks.css :root -- --good: var(--green); --bad: var(--red); --warn: var(--amber); (+ --warning alias). Verified in actual code at C:/Users/user/Desktop/kolmogorov-stack/public/ks.css. The :root "Legacy token aliases" block (lines 107-202) defines --green/--amber/--red/--warning (167-176) and --ks-good/--ks-bad (78-79) but OMITS the unprefixed --good/--bad/--warn. The block's own comment (lines 115-117) states its purpose: "every public HTML page loads ks.css. Putting the aliases here means one edit covers the whole site" — exactly the pattern the fix follows, so this is a genuine omission, not intentional.  Magnitude (verified): 62 account pages use var(--good/bad/warn). 41 of them load ONLY ks.css (all 41 confirmed to link ks.css, none link design-tokens.css) AND use the no-fallback form var(--good)/var(--bad)/var(--warn) (297 such usages site-wide in account/*.html). On those pages the tokens are undefined, so color/background:var(--good) inherits the default ink (#111). overview.html (main account landing) is in this set: loads only ks.css, has 3x var(--good)/4x var(--bad)/2x var(--warn) with no fallback. whats-next.js (loaded by overview.html) SEV_COLOR uses var(--warn) with no fallback — confirmed at lines 16-19. The tokens ARE defined in design-tokens.css (lines 112-114 -> --status-good/warn/bad) which only ~20 of these pages load. So the core defect is real and the fix is correct.  Already implemented? No. No CI guard for undefined CSS tokens exists. --ks-good/--ks-bad (prefixed) exist but the product CSS/HTML uses the UNPREFIXED --good/--bad/--warn, which are absent from ks.css. Truly-broken count is 41, slightly under the finding's "44/60". (2) The design system's status colors are deliberately MUTED per the cool-slate direction: --ks-pos #2d6a48 (muted green), --ks-err #8b2828 (muted red), and critically --ks-warn #56606c is a slate GRAY, not amber. So "fixing" warn shifts text from ink-black to slate-gray — a small visual delta, not a vivid amber. good/bad shifts are more noticeable (ink -> muted green/red). Net: real defect, but "looks broken / accessibility regression" is somewhat overstated; medium-high is fairer than high.  Effort 0.5 days is realistic-to-generous: the actual fix is 3-4 alias lines (--good: var(--green); --bad: var(--red); --warn: var(--amber); + --warning already exists) in the existing block, ~30 min. Optional CI guard adds the remaining time. Users would care: status pills/dots are the core visual language of these cockpit pages, and on the majority of them the ok/warn/bad distinction currently collapses to one color. |

- [high, 0.5d] **Define --good/--bad/--warn status tokens in ks.css (BUG)** — Add to ks.css :root: --good:var(--green); --bad:var(--red); --warn:var(--amber);. 43 pages + whats-next.js reference them with no fallback; only 16/60 load design-tokens.css where they're defined, so status colors collapse to ink on ~44 pages. Optional CI guard for var(--TOKEN) with no :root def. _(public/ks.css)_

## Open questions for the human

- Team compile-credit count is 50 (cards) vs 250 (editorial) and Free is 1 vs 5 — which does the billing backend actually grant? Needed to fix the pricing single-source-of-truth.
- Is the no-code Compile wizard expected to drive a real hosted GPU job now, or stay an explicit 'preview compile' until hosted training infra is funded? Determines whether the account-ui top finding is a 6-day integration or a 0.5-day copy fix.
- Does kolm want a hosted, no-auth, rate-limited free-chat endpoint exposed from the public homepage (cost/abuse exposure), or keep the canned race? Gates the website playground + the create-model capture/live-chat findings.
- Should new injection_classes / cache_hit / estimator_status / matched_rule_id fields go into the Ed25519-SIGNED canonical receipt (schema migration + verifier/SDK churn) or attach as non-signed top-level fields (cheaper, but weaker 'receipt is the proof')? This recurs across gateway, govern, and autopilot findings.
- Confirm /about is a /product rename (not a net-new page) per MEMORY before creating public/about.html, to avoid a duplicate-surface.
- Is the agent/MCP segment a near-term target? Gates the MCP gateway surface and the Warp-style multi-step plan executor.
- Hosted Python/ONNX runtime: acceptable as a dependency for transformer NER (gateway) and IFD/quality-classifier (data-engine), or must everything stay zero-ML-dependency JS with the model paths opt-in only?
- Which Rekor instance for live-receipt anchoring — kolm-operated, public-good Sigstore, or tenant-self-hosted by default? Affects the govern transparency-log finding's trust story.
- Liger-kernel and GLiNER/Presidio/fastText/mergekit/TRL are heavy optional deps — confirm they belong in a [gpu]/optional extra (opt-in) rather than the base install, consistent with the existing honesty contract.
